<s> i've thought of you so much <\s>
<s> but only if you're sure <\s>

<s> give me that ticket i'll send for your things <\s>
<s> obediently she gives him the ticket smiles and goes quietly into the inner room <\s>
<s> miler has entered her face more chinese than ever shows no sign of having seen <\s>
<s> that lady will stay here mrs <\s>
<s> kindly go with this ticket to the cloak room at charing cross station and bring back her luggage in a cab <\s>
<s> she takes the ticket then impassively in case you don't know there's two o them men about the stairs now <\s>
<s> the moment she is gone malise makes a gesture of maniacal fury <\s>
<s> he steals on tiptoe to the outer door and listens <\s>
<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>
<s> transfigured in the last sunlight streaming down the corridor are two men close together listening and consulting secretly <\s>
<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>
<s> scene ii scene ii the same early on a winter afternoon three months later <\s>
<s> the room has now a certain daintiness <\s>
<s> there are curtains over the doors a couch under the window all the books are arranged on shelves <\s>
<s> in small vases over the fireplace are a few violets and chrysanthemums <\s>
<s> malise sits huddled in his armchair drawn close to the fore paper on knee pen in hand <\s>
<s> he looks rather grey and drawn and round his chair is the usual litter <\s>
<s> at the table now nearer to the window clare sits working a typewriter <\s>
<s> she finishes a line puts sheets of paper together makes a note on a card adds some figures and marks the total <\s>
<s> kenneth when this is paid i shall have made two pound seventeen in the three months and saved you about three pounds <\s>
<s> one hundred and seventeen shillings at tenpence a thousand is one hundred and forty thousand words at fourteen hundred words an hour <\s>
<s> it's only just over an hour a day <\s>

<s> going up to him you did sleep last night <\s>
<s> malise nods by this time the day after to morrow the case will be heard and done with <\s>
<s> you're not worrying for me <\s>
<s> except for my poor old dad i don't care a bit <\s>

<s> he is silent a hundred and fifty from the watchfire i know <\s>

<s> i've ad it on my mind a long time to speak to yer <\s>
<s> your comin ere's not done im a bit o good <\s>
<s> i don't want to but what with the worry o this ere divorce suit an you bein a lady an im havin to be so careful of yer and tryin to save not smokin all day like e used an not gettin is two bottles of claret regular an losin his sleep an takin that stuff for it and now this ere last business <\s>
<s> i've seen im sometimes holdin is ead as if it was comin off <\s>
<s> seeing clare wince she goes on with a sort of compassion in her chinese face i can see yer fond of him an i've nothin against yer you don't trouble me a bit but i've been with im eight years we're used to each other and i can't bear to see im not imself really i can't <\s>

<s> now you've ung them curtains you can't elp it <\s>
<s> it's about your divorce case <\s>
<s> this ere watchfire ye see belongs to some fellers that won't ave their men gettin into the papers <\s>

<s> miler has entered her face more chinese than ever shows no sign of having seen <\s>
<s> that lady will stay here mrs <\s>
<s> kindly go with this ticket to the cloak room at charing cross station and bring back her luggage in a cab <\s>
<s> she takes the ticket then impassively in case you don't know there's two o them men about the stairs now <\s>
<s> the moment she is gone malise makes a gesture of maniacal fury <\s>
<s> he steals on tiptoe to the outer door and listens <\s>
<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>
<s> transfigured in the last sunlight streaming down the corridor are two men close together listening and consulting secretly <\s>
<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>

<s> transfigured in the last sunlight streaming down the corridor are two men close together listening and consulting secretly <\s>
<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>
<s> scene ii scene ii the same early on a winter afternoon three months later <\s>
<s> the room has now a certain daintiness <\s>
<s> there are curtains over the doors a couch under the window all the books are arranged on shelves <\s>
<s> in small vases over the fireplace are a few violets and chrysanthemums <\s>
<s> malise sits huddled in his armchair drawn close to the fore paper on knee pen in hand <\s>
<s> he looks rather grey and drawn and round his chair is the usual litter <\s>
<s> at the table now nearer to the window clare sits working a typewriter <\s>
<s> she finishes a line puts sheets of paper together makes a note on a card adds some figures and marks the total <\s>
<s> kenneth when this is paid i shall have made two pound seventeen in the three months and saved you about three pounds <\s>
<s> one hundred and seventeen shillings at tenpence a thousand is one hundred and forty thousand words at fourteen hundred words an hour <\s>
<s> it's only just over an hour a day <\s>
<s> can't you get me more <\s>
<s> malise lifts the hand that holds his pen and lets it fall again <\s>
<s> clare puts the cover on the typewriter and straps it <\s>
<s> shall i pack for you <\s>
<s> he nods can't we have more than three days at the sea <\s>
<s> he shakes his head <\s>
<s> going up to him you did sleep last night <\s>
<s> malise nods by this time the day after to morrow the case will be heard and done with <\s>
<s> you're not worrying for me <\s>
<s> except for my poor old dad i don't care a bit <\s>
<s> malise heaves himself out of the chair and begins pacing up and down <\s>
<s> kenneth do you understand why he doesn't claim damages after what he said that day here <\s>
<s> looking suddenly at him it is true that he doesn't <\s>
<s> but you told me yourself malise <\s>
<s> shrugging no use lying any longer you'd know it tomorrow <\s>
<s> how much am i valued at <\s>
<s> grimly he'll settle it on you <\s>
<s> by one stroke destroys his enemy avenges his honour and gilds his name with generosity <\s>
<s> will you have to pay <\s>
<s> stones yield no blood <\s>
<s> i couldn't even get the costs <\s>
<s> will they make you bankrupt then <\s>
<s> malise nods but that doesn't mean that you won't have your income does it <\s>
<s> malise laughs what is your income kenneth <\s>
<s> he is silent a hundred and fifty from the watchfire i know <\s>
<s> out of five books i have made the sum of forty pounds <\s>
<s> fifty to a hundred pounds a year <\s>
<s> leave me to gnaw my way out child <\s>
<s> clare stands looking at him in distress then goes quickly into the room behind her <\s>
<s> malise takes up his paper and pen <\s>
<s> the paper is quite blank <\s>
<s> feeling his head full of smoke <\s>
<s> he drops paper and pen and crossing to the room on the left goes in <\s>
<s> clare re enters with a small leather box <\s>
<s> she puts it down on her typing table as malise returns followed by mrs <\s>
<s> miler wearing her hat and carrying his overcoat <\s>
<s> put your coat on <\s>
<s> it's a bitter wind <\s>
<s> he puts on the coat clare <\s>
<s> where are you going <\s>
<s> the door closes behind him and mrs <\s>
<s> miler goes up to clare holding out a little blue bottle with a red label nearly full <\s>
<s> you know he's takin this she makes a little motion towards her mouth to make im sleep <\s>
<s> reading the label where was it <\s>
<s> in the bathroom chest o drawers where e keeps is odds and ends <\s>
<s> i was lookin for is garters <\s>
<s> give it to me <\s>
<s> he took it once before <\s>
<s> he must get his sleep <\s>
<s> give it to me <\s>
<s> miler resigns it clare takes the cork out smells then tastes it from her finger <\s>
<s> miler twisting her apron in her hands speaks <\s>
<s> i've ad it on my mind a long time to speak to yer <\s>
<s> your comin ere's not done im a bit o good <\s>
<s> i don't want to but what with the worry o this ere divorce suit an you bein a lady an im havin to be so careful of yer and tryin to save not smokin all day like e used an not gettin is two bottles of claret regular an losin his sleep an takin that stuff for it and now this ere last business <\s>
<s> i've seen im sometimes holdin is ead as if it was comin off <\s>
<s> seeing clare wince she goes on with a sort of compassion in her chinese face i can see yer fond of him an i've nothin against yer you don't trouble me a bit but i've been with im eight years we're used to each other and i can't bear to see im not imself really i can't <\s>
<s> she gives a sadden sniff <\s>
<s> then her emotion passes leaving her as chinese as ever <\s>
<s> this last business what do you mean by that <\s>
<s> if e a'n't told yer i don't know that i've any call to <\s>
<s> her hands twisting very fast well it's to do with this ere watchfire <\s>
<s> one of the men that sees to the writin of it e's an old friend of mr <\s>
<s> malise e come ere this mornin when you was out <\s>
<s> i was doin my work in there she points to the room on the right an the door open so i earl em <\s>
<s> now you've ung them curtains you can't elp it <\s>
<s> it's about your divorce case <\s>
<s> this ere watchfire ye see belongs to some fellers that won't ave their men gettin into the papers <\s>
<s> so this ere friend of mr <\s>
<s> malise very nice e spoke about it if it comes into court e says you'll ave to go e says <\s>
<s> these beggars these dogs these dogs e says they'll oof you out e says <\s>
<s> an i could tell by the sound of his voice e meant it proper upset e was <\s>
<s> that's what i thinks but it don't elp do it <\s>
<s> tain't the circulation e says it's the principle e says and then e starts in swearin horrible <\s>
<s> i've thought of you so much <\s>
<s> but only if you're sure <\s>
<s> he clasps her and kisses her closed eyes and so they stand for a moment till the sound of a latchkey in the door sends them apart <\s>
<s> give me that ticket i'll send for your things <\s>
<s> obediently she gives him the ticket smiles and goes quietly into the inner room <\s>
<s> miler has entered her face more chinese than ever shows no sign of having seen <\s>
<s> that lady will stay here mrs <\s>
<s> kindly go with this ticket to the cloak room at charing cross station and bring back her luggage in a cab <\s>
<s> she takes the ticket then impassively in case you don't know there's two o them men about the stairs now <\s>

<s> he must get his sleep <\s>
<s> give it to me <\s>
<s> miler resigns it clare takes the cork out smells then tastes it from her finger <\s>
<s> miler twisting her apron in her hands speaks <\s>
<s> i've ad it on my mind a long time to speak to yer <\s>
<s> your comin ere's not done im a bit o good <\s>
<s> i don't want to but what with the worry o this ere divorce suit an you bein a lady an im havin to be so careful of yer and tryin to save not smokin all day like e used an not gettin is two bottles of claret regular an losin his sleep an takin that stuff for it and now this ere last business <\s>
<s> i've seen im sometimes holdin is ead as if it was comin off <\s>
<s> seeing clare wince she goes on with a sort of compassion in her chinese face i can see yer fond of him an i've nothin against yer you don't trouble me a bit but i've been with im eight years we're used to each other and i can't bear to see im not imself really i can't <\s>
<s> she gives a sadden sniff <\s>
<s> then her emotion passes leaving her as chinese as ever <\s>
<s> this last business what do you mean by that <\s>
<s> if e a'n't told yer i don't know that i've any call to <\s>
<s> her hands twisting very fast well it's to do with this ere watchfire <\s>
<s> one of the men that sees to the writin of it e's an old friend of mr <\s>
<s> malise e come ere this mornin when you was out <\s>
<s> i was doin my work in there she points to the room on the right an the door open so i earl em <\s>
<s> now you've ung them curtains you can't elp it <\s>
<s> it's about your divorce case <\s>
<s> this ere watchfire ye see belongs to some fellers that won't ave their men gettin into the papers <\s>
<s> so this ere friend of mr <\s>
<s> malise very nice e spoke about it if it comes into court e says you'll ave to go e says <\s>
<s> these beggars these dogs these dogs e says they'll oof you out e says <\s>
<s> an i could tell by the sound of his voice e meant it proper upset e was <\s>
<s> that's what i thinks but it don't elp do it <\s>
<s> tain't the circulation e says it's the principle e says and then e starts in swearin horrible <\s>
<s> i've thought of you so much <\s>
<s> but only if you're sure <\s>
<s> he clasps her and kisses her closed eyes and so they stand for a moment till the sound of a latchkey in the door sends them apart <\s>
<s> give me that ticket i'll send for your things <\s>
<s> obediently she gives him the ticket smiles and goes quietly into the inner room <\s>
<s> miler has entered her face more chinese than ever shows no sign of having seen <\s>
<s> that lady will stay here mrs <\s>
<s> kindly go with this ticket to the cloak room at charing cross station and bring back her luggage in a cab <\s>
<s> she takes the ticket then impassively in case you don't know there's two o them men about the stairs now <\s>
<s> the moment she is gone malise makes a gesture of maniacal fury <\s>
<s> he steals on tiptoe to the outer door and listens <\s>
<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>
<s> transfigured in the last sunlight streaming down the corridor are two men close together listening and consulting secretly <\s>
<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>
<s> scene ii scene ii the same early on a winter afternoon three months later <\s>
<s> the room has now a certain daintiness <\s>

<s> kenneth when this is paid i shall have made two pound seventeen in the three months and saved you about three pounds <\s>
<s> one hundred and seventeen shillings at tenpence a thousand is one hundred and forty thousand words at fourteen hundred words an hour <\s>
<s> it's only just over an hour a day <\s>
<s> can't you get me more <\s>
<s> malise lifts the hand that holds his pen and lets it fall again <\s>
<s> clare puts the cover on the typewriter and straps it <\s>
<s> shall i pack for you <\s>
<s> he nods can't we have more than three days at the sea <\s>
<s> he shakes his head <\s>
<s> going up to him you did sleep last night <\s>
<s> malise nods by this time the day after to morrow the case will be heard and done with <\s>
<s> you're not worrying for me <\s>
<s> except for my poor old dad i don't care a bit <\s>
<s> malise heaves himself out of the chair and begins pacing up and down <\s>
<s> kenneth do you understand why he doesn't claim damages after what he said that day here <\s>
<s> looking suddenly at him it is true that he doesn't <\s>
<s> but you told me yourself malise <\s>
<s> shrugging no use lying any longer you'd know it tomorrow <\s>
<s> how much am i valued at <\s>
<s> grimly he'll settle it on you <\s>
<s> by one stroke destroys his enemy avenges his honour and gilds his name with generosity <\s>
<s> will you have to pay <\s>
<s> stones yield no blood <\s>
<s> i couldn't even get the costs <\s>
<s> will they make you bankrupt then <\s>
<s> malise nods but that doesn't mean that you won't have your income does it <\s>
<s> malise laughs what is your income kenneth <\s>
<s> he is silent a hundred and fifty from the watchfire i know <\s>
<s> out of five books i have made the sum of forty pounds <\s>
<s> fifty to a hundred pounds a year <\s>
<s> leave me to gnaw my way out child <\s>
<s> clare stands looking at him in distress then goes quickly into the room behind her <\s>
<s> malise takes up his paper and pen <\s>
<s> the paper is quite blank <\s>
<s> feeling his head full of smoke <\s>
<s> he drops paper and pen and crossing to the room on the left goes in <\s>
<s> clare re enters with a small leather box <\s>
<s> she puts it down on her typing table as malise returns followed by mrs <\s>
<s> miler wearing her hat and carrying his overcoat <\s>
<s> put your coat on <\s>
<s> it's a bitter wind <\s>
<s> he puts on the coat clare <\s>
<s> where are you going <\s>
<s> the door closes behind him and mrs <\s>
<s> miler goes up to clare holding out a little blue bottle with a red label nearly full <\s>
<s> you know he's takin this she makes a little motion towards her mouth to make im sleep <\s>
<s> reading the label where was it <\s>
<s> in the bathroom chest o drawers where e keeps is odds and ends <\s>
<s> i was lookin for is garters <\s>
<s> give it to me <\s>
<s> he took it once before <\s>
<s> he must get his sleep <\s>
<s> give it to me <\s>
<s> miler resigns it clare takes the cork out smells then tastes it from her finger <\s>
<s> miler twisting her apron in her hands speaks <\s>
<s> i've ad it on my mind a long time to speak to yer <\s>
<s> your comin ere's not done im a bit o good <\s>
<s> i don't want to but what with the worry o this ere divorce suit an you bein a lady an im havin to be so careful of yer and tryin to save not smokin all day like e used an not gettin is two bottles of claret regular an losin his sleep an takin that stuff for it and now this ere last business <\s>
<s> i've seen im sometimes holdin is ead as if it was comin off <\s>
<s> seeing clare wince she goes on with a sort of compassion in her chinese face i can see yer fond of him an i've nothin against yer you don't trouble me a bit but i've been with im eight years we're used to each other and i can't bear to see im not imself really i can't <\s>
<s> she gives a sadden sniff <\s>
<s> then her emotion passes leaving her as chinese as ever <\s>
<s> this last business what do you mean by that <\s>
<s> if e a'n't told yer i don't know that i've any call to <\s>
<s> her hands twisting very fast well it's to do with this ere watchfire <\s>
<s> one of the men that sees to the writin of it e's an old friend of mr <\s>
<s> malise e come ere this mornin when you was out <\s>
<s> i was doin my work in there she points to the room on the right an the door open so i earl em <\s>
<s> now you've ung them curtains you can't elp it <\s>
<s> it's about your divorce case <\s>
<s> this ere watchfire ye see belongs to some fellers that won't ave their men gettin into the papers <\s>
<s> so this ere friend of mr <\s>
<s> malise very nice e spoke about it if it comes into court e says you'll ave to go e says <\s>
<s> these beggars these dogs these dogs e says they'll oof you out e says <\s>
<s> an i could tell by the sound of his voice e meant it proper upset e was <\s>
<s> that's what i thinks but it don't elp do it <\s>
<s> tain't the circulation e says it's the principle e says and then e starts in swearin horrible <\s>
<s> i've thought of you so much <\s>
<s> but only if you're sure <\s>
<s> he clasps her and kisses her closed eyes and so they stand for a moment till the sound of a latchkey in the door sends them apart <\s>
<s> give me that ticket i'll send for your things <\s>
<s> obediently she gives him the ticket smiles and goes quietly into the inner room <\s>
<s> miler has entered her face more chinese than ever shows no sign of having seen <\s>
<s> that lady will stay here mrs <\s>
<s> kindly go with this ticket to the cloak room at charing cross station and bring back her luggage in a cab <\s>
<s> she takes the ticket then impassively in case you don't know there's two o them men about the stairs now <\s>
<s> the moment she is gone malise makes a gesture of maniacal fury <\s>
<s> he steals on tiptoe to the outer door and listens <\s>
<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>
<s> transfigured in the last sunlight streaming down the corridor are two men close together listening and consulting secretly <\s>
<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>

<s> miler has entered her face more chinese than ever shows no sign of having seen <\s>
<s> that lady will stay here mrs <\s>
<s> kindly go with this ticket to the cloak room at charing cross station and bring back her luggage in a cab <\s>
<s> she takes the ticket then impassively in case you don't know there's two o them men about the stairs now <\s>
<s> the moment she is gone malise makes a gesture of maniacal fury <\s>
<s> he steals on tiptoe to the outer door and listens <\s>
<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>
<s> transfigured in the last sunlight streaming down the corridor are two men close together listening and consulting secretly <\s>
<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>

<s> your comin ere's not done im a bit o good <\s>
<s> i don't want to but what with the worry o this ere divorce suit an you bein a lady an im havin to be so careful of yer and tryin to save not smokin all day like e used an not gettin is two bottles of claret regular an losin his sleep an takin that stuff for it and now this ere last business <\s>
<s> i've seen im sometimes holdin is ead as if it was comin off <\s>
<s> seeing clare wince she goes on with a sort of compassion in her chinese face i can see yer fond of him an i've nothin against yer you don't trouble me a bit but i've been with im eight years we're used to each other and i can't bear to see im not imself really i can't <\s>

<s> the moment she is gone malise makes a gesture of maniacal fury <\s>

<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>

<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>

<s> miler has entered her face more chinese than ever shows no sign of having seen <\s>
<s> that lady will stay here mrs <\s>
<s> kindly go with this ticket to the cloak room at charing cross station and bring back her luggage in a cab <\s>
<s> she takes the ticket then impassively in case you don't know there's two o them men about the stairs now <\s>
<s> the moment she is gone malise makes a gesture of maniacal fury <\s>
<s> he steals on tiptoe to the outer door and listens <\s>
<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>
<s> transfigured in the last sunlight streaming down the corridor are two men close together listening and consulting secretly <\s>
<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>
<s> scene ii scene ii the same early on a winter afternoon three months later <\s>
<s> the room has now a certain daintiness <\s>
<s> there are curtains over the doors a couch under the window all the books are arranged on shelves <\s>
<s> in small vases over the fireplace are a few violets and chrysanthemums <\s>

<s> he looks rather grey and drawn and round his chair is the usual litter <\s>

<s> but only if you're sure <\s>

<s> give me that ticket i'll send for your things <\s>
<s> obediently she gives him the ticket smiles and goes quietly into the inner room <\s>
<s> miler has entered her face more chinese than ever shows no sign of having seen <\s>
<s> that lady will stay here mrs <\s>
<s> kindly go with this ticket to the cloak room at charing cross station and bring back her luggage in a cab <\s>
<s> she takes the ticket then impassively in case you don't know there's two o them men about the stairs now <\s>
<s> the moment she is gone malise makes a gesture of maniacal fury <\s>
<s> he steals on tiptoe to the outer door and listens <\s>
<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>
<s> transfigured in the last sunlight streaming down the corridor are two men close together listening and consulting secretly <\s>
<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>
<s> scene ii scene ii the same early on a winter afternoon three months later <\s>
<s> the room has now a certain daintiness <\s>
<s> there are curtains over the doors a couch under the window all the books are arranged on shelves <\s>
<s> in small vases over the fireplace are a few violets and chrysanthemums <\s>
<s> malise sits huddled in his armchair drawn close to the fore paper on knee pen in hand <\s>
<s> he looks rather grey and drawn and round his chair is the usual litter <\s>
<s> at the table now nearer to the window clare sits working a typewriter <\s>
<s> she finishes a line puts sheets of paper together makes a note on a card adds some figures and marks the total <\s>
<s> kenneth when this is paid i shall have made two pound seventeen in the three months and saved you about three pounds <\s>
<s> one hundred and seventeen shillings at tenpence a thousand is one hundred and forty thousand words at fourteen hundred words an hour <\s>

<s> your comin ere's not done im a bit o good <\s>
<s> i don't want to but what with the worry o this ere divorce suit an you bein a lady an im havin to be so careful of yer and tryin to save not smokin all day like e used an not gettin is two bottles of claret regular an losin his sleep an takin that stuff for it and now this ere last business <\s>
<s> i've seen im sometimes holdin is ead as if it was comin off <\s>
<s> seeing clare wince she goes on with a sort of compassion in her chinese face i can see yer fond of him an i've nothin against yer you don't trouble me a bit but i've been with im eight years we're used to each other and i can't bear to see im not imself really i can't <\s>

<s> that lady will stay here mrs <\s>

<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>

<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>

<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>
<s> transfigured in the last sunlight streaming down the corridor are two men close together listening and consulting secretly <\s>
<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>
<s> scene ii scene ii the same early on a winter afternoon three months later <\s>
<s> the room has now a certain daintiness <\s>
<s> there are curtains over the doors a couch under the window all the books are arranged on shelves <\s>
<s> in small vases over the fireplace are a few violets and chrysanthemums <\s>
<s> malise sits huddled in his armchair drawn close to the fore paper on knee pen in hand <\s>
<s> he looks rather grey and drawn and round his chair is the usual litter <\s>
<s> at the table now nearer to the window clare sits working a typewriter <\s>
<s> she finishes a line puts sheets of paper together makes a note on a card adds some figures and marks the total <\s>
<s> kenneth when this is paid i shall have made two pound seventeen in the three months and saved you about three pounds <\s>
<s> one hundred and seventeen shillings at tenpence a thousand is one hundred and forty thousand words at fourteen hundred words an hour <\s>
<s> it's only just over an hour a day <\s>
<s> can't you get me more <\s>
<s> malise lifts the hand that holds his pen and lets it fall again <\s>
<s> clare puts the cover on the typewriter and straps it <\s>
<s> shall i pack for you <\s>
<s> he nods can't we have more than three days at the sea <\s>
<s> he shakes his head <\s>
<s> going up to him you did sleep last night <\s>
<s> malise nods by this time the day after to morrow the case will be heard and done with <\s>
<s> you're not worrying for me <\s>
<s> except for my poor old dad i don't care a bit <\s>
<s> malise heaves himself out of the chair and begins pacing up and down <\s>
<s> kenneth do you understand why he doesn't claim damages after what he said that day here <\s>
<s> looking suddenly at him it is true that he doesn't <\s>
<s> but you told me yourself malise <\s>
<s> shrugging no use lying any longer you'd know it tomorrow <\s>
<s> how much am i valued at <\s>
<s> grimly he'll settle it on you <\s>
<s> by one stroke destroys his enemy avenges his honour and gilds his name with generosity <\s>
<s> will you have to pay <\s>
<s> stones yield no blood <\s>
<s> i couldn't even get the costs <\s>
<s> will they make you bankrupt then <\s>
<s> malise nods but that doesn't mean that you won't have your income does it <\s>
<s> malise laughs what is your income kenneth <\s>
<s> he is silent a hundred and fifty from the watchfire i know <\s>
<s> out of five books i have made the sum of forty pounds <\s>
<s> fifty to a hundred pounds a year <\s>
<s> leave me to gnaw my way out child <\s>
<s> clare stands looking at him in distress then goes quickly into the room behind her <\s>
<s> malise takes up his paper and pen <\s>
<s> the paper is quite blank <\s>
<s> feeling his head full of smoke <\s>
<s> he drops paper and pen and crossing to the room on the left goes in <\s>
<s> clare re enters with a small leather box <\s>
<s> she puts it down on her typing table as malise returns followed by mrs <\s>
<s> miler wearing her hat and carrying his overcoat <\s>
<s> put your coat on <\s>
<s> it's a bitter wind <\s>
<s> he puts on the coat clare <\s>
<s> where are you going <\s>
<s> the door closes behind him and mrs <\s>
<s> miler goes up to clare holding out a little blue bottle with a red label nearly full <\s>
<s> you know he's takin this she makes a little motion towards her mouth to make im sleep <\s>
<s> reading the label where was it <\s>
<s> in the bathroom chest o drawers where e keeps is odds and ends <\s>
<s> i was lookin for is garters <\s>
<s> give it to me <\s>
<s> he took it once before <\s>
<s> he must get his sleep <\s>
<s> give it to me <\s>
<s> miler resigns it clare takes the cork out smells then tastes it from her finger <\s>
<s> miler twisting her apron in her hands speaks <\s>
<s> i've ad it on my mind a long time to speak to yer <\s>
<s> your comin ere's not done im a bit o good <\s>
<s> i don't want to but what with the worry o this ere divorce suit an you bein a lady an im havin to be so careful of yer and tryin to save not smokin all day like e used an not gettin is two bottles of claret regular an losin his sleep an takin that stuff for it and now this ere last business <\s>
<s> i've seen im sometimes holdin is ead as if it was comin off <\s>
<s> seeing clare wince she goes on with a sort of compassion in her chinese face i can see yer fond of him an i've nothin against yer you don't trouble me a bit but i've been with im eight years we're used to each other and i can't bear to see im not imself really i can't <\s>
<s> she gives a sadden sniff <\s>
<s> then her emotion passes leaving her as chinese as ever <\s>
<s> this last business what do you mean by that <\s>
<s> if e a'n't told yer i don't know that i've any call to <\s>
<s> her hands twisting very fast well it's to do with this ere watchfire <\s>
<s> one of the men that sees to the writin of it e's an old friend of mr <\s>
<s> malise e come ere this mornin when you was out <\s>
<s> i was doin my work in there she points to the room on the right an the door open so i earl em <\s>
<s> now you've ung them curtains you can't elp it <\s>
<s> it's about your divorce case <\s>
<s> this ere watchfire ye see belongs to some fellers that won't ave their men gettin into the papers <\s>
<s> so this ere friend of mr <\s>
<s> malise very nice e spoke about it if it comes into court e says you'll ave to go e says <\s>
<s> these beggars these dogs these dogs e says they'll oof you out e says <\s>
<s> an i could tell by the sound of his voice e meant it proper upset e was <\s>
<s> that's what i thinks but it don't elp do it <\s>
<s> tain't the circulation e says it's the principle e says and then e starts in swearin horrible <\s>
<s> i've thought of you so much <\s>
<s> but only if you're sure <\s>
<s> he clasps her and kisses her closed eyes and so they stand for a moment till the sound of a latchkey in the door sends them apart <\s>
<s> give me that ticket i'll send for your things <\s>
<s> obediently she gives him the ticket smiles and goes quietly into the inner room <\s>
<s> miler has entered her face more chinese than ever shows no sign of having seen <\s>
<s> that lady will stay here mrs <\s>
<s> kindly go with this ticket to the cloak room at charing cross station and bring back her luggage in a cab <\s>
<s> she takes the ticket then impassively in case you don't know there's two o them men about the stairs now <\s>

<s> i've ad it on my mind a long time to speak to yer <\s>
<s> your comin ere's not done im a bit o good <\s>
<s> i don't want to but what with the worry o this ere divorce suit an you bein a lady an im havin to be so careful of yer and tryin to save not smokin all day like e used an not gettin is two bottles of claret regular an losin his sleep an takin that stuff for it and now this ere last business <\s>
<s> i've seen im sometimes holdin is ead as if it was comin off <\s>
<s> seeing clare wince she goes on with a sort of compassion in her chinese face i can see yer fond of him an i've nothin against yer you don't trouble me a bit but i've been with im eight years we're used to each other and i can't bear to see im not imself really i can't <\s>
<s> she gives a sadden sniff <\s>
<s> then her emotion passes leaving her as chinese as ever <\s>

<s> if e a'n't told yer i don't know that i've any call to <\s>
<s> her hands twisting very fast well it's to do with this ere watchfire <\s>

<s> malise e come ere this mornin when you was out <\s>
<s> i was doin my work in there she points to the room on the right an the door open so i earl em <\s>
<s> now you've ung them curtains you can't elp it <\s>
<s> it's about your divorce case <\s>
<s> this ere watchfire ye see belongs to some fellers that won't ave their men gettin into the papers <\s>
<s> so this ere friend of mr <\s>
<s> malise very nice e spoke about it if it comes into court e says you'll ave to go e says <\s>
<s> these beggars these dogs these dogs e says they'll oof you out e says <\s>
<s> an i could tell by the sound of his voice e meant it proper upset e was <\s>
<s> that's what i thinks but it don't elp do it <\s>

<s> i've thought of you so much <\s>
<s> but only if you're sure <\s>

<s> give me that ticket i'll send for your things <\s>
<s> obediently she gives him the ticket smiles and goes quietly into the inner room <\s>
<s> miler has entered her face more chinese than ever shows no sign of having seen <\s>
<s> that lady will stay here mrs <\s>
<s> kindly go with this ticket to the cloak room at charing cross station and bring back her luggage in a cab <\s>
<s> she takes the ticket then impassively in case you don't know there's two o them men about the stairs now <\s>
<s> the moment she is gone malise makes a gesture of maniacal fury <\s>
<s> he steals on tiptoe to the outer door and listens <\s>
<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>
<s> transfigured in the last sunlight streaming down the corridor are two men close together listening and consulting secretly <\s>
<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>

<s> she finishes a line puts sheets of paper together makes a note on a card adds some figures and marks the total <\s>
<s> kenneth when this is paid i shall have made two pound seventeen in the three months and saved you about three pounds <\s>
<s> one hundred and seventeen shillings at tenpence a thousand is one hundred and forty thousand words at fourteen hundred words an hour <\s>
<s> it's only just over an hour a day <\s>
<s> can't you get me more <\s>
<s> malise lifts the hand that holds his pen and lets it fall again <\s>
<s> clare puts the cover on the typewriter and straps it <\s>
<s> shall i pack for you <\s>
<s> he nods can't we have more than three days at the sea <\s>
<s> he shakes his head <\s>
<s> going up to him you did sleep last night <\s>
<s> malise nods by this time the day after to morrow the case will be heard and done with <\s>
<s> you're not worrying for me <\s>
<s> except for my poor old dad i don't care a bit <\s>
<s> malise heaves himself out of the chair and begins pacing up and down <\s>
<s> kenneth do you understand why he doesn't claim damages after what he said that day here <\s>
<s> looking suddenly at him it is true that he doesn't <\s>
<s> but you told me yourself malise <\s>
<s> shrugging no use lying any longer you'd know it tomorrow <\s>
<s> how much am i valued at <\s>
<s> grimly he'll settle it on you <\s>
<s> by one stroke destroys his enemy avenges his honour and gilds his name with generosity <\s>
<s> will you have to pay <\s>
<s> stones yield no blood <\s>
<s> i couldn't even get the costs <\s>
<s> will they make you bankrupt then <\s>
<s> malise nods but that doesn't mean that you won't have your income does it <\s>
<s> malise laughs what is your income kenneth <\s>
<s> he is silent a hundred and fifty from the watchfire i know <\s>
<s> out of five books i have made the sum of forty pounds <\s>
<s> fifty to a hundred pounds a year <\s>
<s> leave me to gnaw my way out child <\s>
<s> clare stands looking at him in distress then goes quickly into the room behind her <\s>
<s> malise takes up his paper and pen <\s>
<s> the paper is quite blank <\s>
<s> feeling his head full of smoke <\s>
<s> he drops paper and pen and crossing to the room on the left goes in <\s>
<s> clare re enters with a small leather box <\s>
<s> she puts it down on her typing table as malise returns followed by mrs <\s>
<s> miler wearing her hat and carrying his overcoat <\s>
<s> put your coat on <\s>
<s> it's a bitter wind <\s>
<s> he puts on the coat clare <\s>
<s> where are you going <\s>
<s> the door closes behind him and mrs <\s>
<s> miler goes up to clare holding out a little blue bottle with a red label nearly full <\s>
<s> you know he's takin this she makes a little motion towards her mouth to make im sleep <\s>
<s> reading the label where was it <\s>
<s> in the bathroom chest o drawers where e keeps is odds and ends <\s>
<s> i was lookin for is garters <\s>
<s> give it to me <\s>
<s> he took it once before <\s>
<s> he must get his sleep <\s>
<s> give it to me <\s>
<s> miler resigns it clare takes the cork out smells then tastes it from her finger <\s>
<s> miler twisting her apron in her hands speaks <\s>
<s> i've ad it on my mind a long time to speak to yer <\s>
<s> your comin ere's not done im a bit o good <\s>
<s> i don't want to but what with the worry o this ere divorce suit an you bein a lady an im havin to be so careful of yer and tryin to save not smokin all day like e used an not gettin is two bottles of claret regular an losin his sleep an takin that stuff for it and now this ere last business <\s>
<s> i've seen im sometimes holdin is ead as if it was comin off <\s>
<s> seeing clare wince she goes on with a sort of compassion in her chinese face i can see yer fond of him an i've nothin against yer you don't trouble me a bit but i've been with im eight years we're used to each other and i can't bear to see im not imself really i can't <\s>
<s> she gives a sadden sniff <\s>
<s> then her emotion passes leaving her as chinese as ever <\s>
<s> this last business what do you mean by that <\s>
<s> if e a'n't told yer i don't know that i've any call to <\s>
<s> her hands twisting very fast well it's to do with this ere watchfire <\s>
<s> one of the men that sees to the writin of it e's an old friend of mr <\s>
<s> malise e come ere this mornin when you was out <\s>
<s> i was doin my work in there she points to the room on the right an the door open so i earl em <\s>
<s> now you've ung them curtains you can't elp it <\s>
<s> it's about your divorce case <\s>
<s> this ere watchfire ye see belongs to some fellers that won't ave their men gettin into the papers <\s>
<s> so this ere friend of mr <\s>
<s> malise very nice e spoke about it if it comes into court e says you'll ave to go e says <\s>
<s> these beggars these dogs these dogs e says they'll oof you out e says <\s>
<s> an i could tell by the sound of his voice e meant it proper upset e was <\s>
<s> that's what i thinks but it don't elp do it <\s>
<s> tain't the circulation e says it's the principle e says and then e starts in swearin horrible <\s>
<s> i've thought of you so much <\s>
<s> but only if you're sure <\s>
<s> he clasps her and kisses her closed eyes and so they stand for a moment till the sound of a latchkey in the door sends them apart <\s>
<s> give me that ticket i'll send for your things <\s>
<s> obediently she gives him the ticket smiles and goes quietly into the inner room <\s>
<s> miler has entered her face more chinese than ever shows no sign of having seen <\s>
<s> that lady will stay here mrs <\s>
<s> kindly go with this ticket to the cloak room at charing cross station and bring back her luggage in a cab <\s>
<s> she takes the ticket then impassively in case you don't know there's two o them men about the stairs now <\s>
<s> the moment she is gone malise makes a gesture of maniacal fury <\s>
<s> he steals on tiptoe to the outer door and listens <\s>
<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>
<s> transfigured in the last sunlight streaming down the corridor are two men close together listening and consulting secretly <\s>
<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>

<s> miler has entered her face more chinese than ever shows no sign of having seen <\s>
<s> that lady will stay here mrs <\s>
<s> kindly go with this ticket to the cloak room at charing cross station and bring back her luggage in a cab <\s>
<s> she takes the ticket then impassively in case you don't know there's two o them men about the stairs now <\s>
<s> the moment she is gone malise makes a gesture of maniacal fury <\s>
<s> he steals on tiptoe to the outer door and listens <\s>
<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>
<s> transfigured in the last sunlight streaming down the corridor are two men close together listening and consulting secretly <\s>
<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>

<s> your comin ere's not done im a bit o good <\s>
<s> i don't want to but what with the worry o this ere divorce suit an you bein a lady an im havin to be so careful of yer and tryin to save not smokin all day like e used an not gettin is two bottles of claret regular an losin his sleep an takin that stuff for it and now this ere last business <\s>
<s> i've seen im sometimes holdin is ead as if it was comin off <\s>
<s> seeing clare wince she goes on with a sort of compassion in her chinese face i can see yer fond of him an i've nothin against yer you don't trouble me a bit but i've been with im eight years we're used to each other and i can't bear to see im not imself really i can't <\s>

<s> the moment she is gone malise makes a gesture of maniacal fury <\s>

<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>

<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>

<s> miler has entered her face more chinese than ever shows no sign of having seen <\s>
<s> that lady will stay here mrs <\s>
<s> kindly go with this ticket to the cloak room at charing cross station and bring back her luggage in a cab <\s>
<s> she takes the ticket then impassively in case you don't know there's two o them men about the stairs now <\s>
<s> the moment she is gone malise makes a gesture of maniacal fury <\s>
<s> he steals on tiptoe to the outer door and listens <\s>
<s> then placing his hand on the knob he turns it without noise and wrenches back the door <\s>
<s> transfigured in the last sunlight streaming down the corridor are two men close together listening and consulting secretly <\s>
<s> with strange almost noiseless ferocity you've run her to earth your job's done <\s>
<s> and in their faces he slams the door curtain <\s>
<s> scene ii scene ii the same early on a winter afternoon three months later <\s>
<s> the room has now a certain daintiness <\s>
<s> there are curtains over the doors a couch under the window all the books are arranged on shelves <\s>
<s> in small vases over the fireplace are a few violets and chrysanthemums <\s>

<s> he looks rather grey and drawn and round his chair is the usual litter <\s>
